<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:center">The Toronto Stock Exchange</td></tr> </table><p style="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Indicate by check mark whether the registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter) or Rule <span style="white-space:nowrap">12b-2</span> of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#167;240.12b-2</span> of this chapter).</p><p style="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Emerging growth company&#8194;<ix:nonNumeric contextRef="duration_2026-01-29_to_2026-01-29" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" format="ixt:fixed-true" id="ixv-330">&#9746;</ix:nonNumeric></p><p style="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section&#160;13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#8194;<ix:nonNumeric contextRef="duration_2026-01-29_to_2026-01-29" name="dei:EntityExTransitionPeriod" format="ixt:fixed-false" id="ixv-331">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <div style="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</div> <div style="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</div></div></div><p style="page-break-before:always"></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
<table style="border-collapse:collapse; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border-spacing:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top;text-align:left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;5.02.</span></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"><p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.</p></td></tr> </table><p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&#160;29, 2026, the board of directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of <span style="white-space:nowrap">i-80</span> Gold Corp. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) appointed Ronald Butler Jr., Michael Jalonen and Steven Yopps to the Board, effective February&#160;1, 2026.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effective February&#160;1, 2026, Mr.&#160;Butler and Mr.&#160;Jalonen were appointed to the Audit Committee of the Board, Mr.&#160;Butler and Mr.&#160;Yopps were appointed to the Compensation Committee of the Board, and Mr.&#160;Yopps and Mr.&#160;Jalonen were appointed to the Technical, Safety and Sustainability Committee of the Board.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">There are no arrangements or understandings between Mr.&#160;Butler, Mr.&#160;Jalonen or Mr.&#160;Yopps and any other persons pursuant to which they were selected as a director. Mr.&#160;Butler, Mr.&#160;Jalonen and Mr.&#160;Yopps do not have direct or indirect material interests in any currently proposed transaction to which the Company was, or is to be, a participant, nor has either Mr.&#160;Butler, Mr.&#160;Jalonen or Mr.&#160;Yopps had a direct or indirect material interest in any transactions since the beginning of the Company&#8217;s last fiscal year.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mr.&#160;Butler, Mr.&#160;Jalonen and Mr.&#160;Yopps will be compensated for their service on the Board consistent with the Company&#8217;s other <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-employee</span> directors. They each will receive an annual retainer in the amount of $55,000 and an annual award of deferred share units with an approximate value of $75,000. Each grant of deferred share units will vest in accordance with the terms set out in the Company&#8217;s omnibus share incentive plan.</p><p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Ronald Butler Jr. </span></p><p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ronald Butler Jr. is a Certified Public Accountant (CPA) with more than 30 years of experience in audit, financial and strategic planning, operational excellence, digital transformation, and corporate governance across industries including mining and metals, energy, technology, and consumer products. Mr.&#160;Butler spent 29 years with Ernst&#160;&amp; Young LLP (EY) in Arizona, most recently serving as Managing Partner from 2008 until his retirement in 2024. From 2022 to 2024, he also served as EY&#8217;s U.S. Mining&#160;&amp; Metals Leader, where he led national strategy and drove client and business growth, advising major mining companies such as Freeport-McMoRan and Newmont Corporation. As Managing Partner, Mr.&#160;Butler led EY Arizona&#8217;s growth initiatives and strategic ventures, including public-sector programs focused on cost reduction, grants management, real estate optimization, and technology enablement. He also served on the Executive Committee for the City of Phoenix&#8217;s US$500&#160;million General Obligation Bond Program and was a senior member of EY&#8217;s West Region Executive Leadership Team. During his tenure, he oversaw more than 500 professionals and advised a broad range of midsize and multinational public and private companies. Mr.&#160;Butler holds a BSc in Accountancy from the University of Arizona.</p><p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Michael Jalonen </span></p><p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Michael Jalonen is a Chartered Financial Analyst (CFA) with nearly 40 years of mining and capital markets experience, including over 30 years as a highly respected mining analyst at Bank of America Securities (BofA). He served as Managing Director and North American Senior Precious Metals Research Analyst from 1989 until his retirement in 2022 and was consistently ranked among the leading mining analysts in North America. In this role, Mr.&#160;Jalonen led coverage and investment recommendations for 30 senior and intermediate precious metals producers, as well as royalty and streaming companies. He developed detailed operating and financial models, performed valuation analyses, and authored numerous thematic industry reports. Prior to that, Mr.&#160;Jalonen served as Global Coordinator for BofA&#8217;s Metals, Mining&#160;&amp; Steel Research Team, overseeing a global group of analysts, publishing thematic research on precious and base metals, and organizing the firm&#8217;s flagship global mining conference. He began his career as a geologist. Mr.&#160;Jalonen holds an MBA in Finance from the DeGroote School of Business and a BSc (Hons) in Geology from the University of Windsor.</p><p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Steven Yopps </span></p><p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Steven Yopps is a metallurgical engineer and accomplished mining executive with more than 35 years of operational, technical, project development, and regulatory experience across Nevada&#8217;s premier gold districts. His career spans senior roles at AngloGold Ashanti, Nevada Gold Mines, and Barrick Mining, where he led large-scale autoclave, roaster, and refractory processing operations, advanced complex feasibility studies, and executed district-level growth strategies that transformed regional mining portfolios.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Most recently, Mr.&#160;Yopps served as Vice President of Nevada Projects for AngloGold Ashanti from 2021 through to his retirement in 2025. In this role, he led technical and exploration teams who were responsible for growing the</p></div></div><p style="page-break-before:always"></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto"><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"> Nevada resource base, advancing the feasibility study and NEPA permitting for the North Bullfrog project, and supporting the integration of acquisitions within the Beatty district to establish a <span style="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</span> mining district in southern Nevada. Previously, Mr.&#160;Yopps was Manager of Growth Projects for Nevada Gold Mines (&#8220;NGM&#8221;) from 2019 to 2021, where he led the long-term processing and refractory ore transportation strategy following the Newmont-Barrick joint venture, multiple <span style="white-space:nowrap">pre-feasibility</span> studies at Cortez, and refractory ore research and development programs. He has authored peer-reviewed research on Carlin-type refractory gold processing and pressure oxidation technologies.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prior to his role at NGM, he spent more than 25 years in senior technical and operational roles, including serving as General Manager of the Ruby Hill Mine (currently <span style="white-space:nowrap">i-80</span> Gold&#8217;s wholly owned Ruby Hill property) and managing Goldstrike&#8217;s autoclave, roaster, and mill facilities for more than a decade, delivering <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</span></span> safety and operational performance. Mr.&#160;Yopps holds a BSc and MSc in Metallurgical Engineering from the Colorado School of Mines and is a Qualified Person recognized by the Mining&#160;&amp; Metallurgical Society of America.</p><p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g103403dsp001.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT> Gold Strengthens Board of Directors with the Addition
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>of Ronald Butler Jr., Michael Jalonen, and Steven Yopps </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>TORONTO, ON, January</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;29, 2026</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;&#8211; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT> GOLD CORP. (TSX:IAU) (NYSE
American:IAUX) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;i-80</FONT> Gold&#8221;, or the &#8220;Company&#8221;)</B><B></B>&nbsp;is pleased to announce the appointment of Ronald Butler Jr., Michael Jalonen and Steven Yopps to its Board as independent
directors, effective February&nbsp;1, 2026. These additions strengthen the Company&#8217;s governance with deep experience in mining operations, finance, mineral processing, and capital markets. This collective experience will support <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT> Gold in achieving its growth strategy in Nevada. Following their appointments, the Board will be comprised of nine members. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8220;Ron, Mike, and Steve each bring highly relevant experience and proven track records across their respective fields, including financial leadership,
deep capital markets knowledge, and autoclave and refractory processing expertise, making them strong additions to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT> Gold&#8217;s Board of Directors,&#8221; said Ron Clayton, Chairman of the Board. &#8220;I
am confident their expertise will provide valuable insight and guidance as the Company executes its development plan spanning five gold projects and the refurbishment of our Lone Tree autoclave processing facility to create long-term value for
shareholders. These appointments reflect our ongoing effort to ensure that the Board maintains the technical, financial, and strategic skills and experience required to support the Company as we advance toward becoming a leading <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-tier</FONT> gold producer in Nevada. On behalf of the Board, we are pleased to welcome three directors of this caliber.&#8221; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Ronald Butler Jr. </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ronald Butler Jr. is a
Certified Public Accountant (CPA) with more than 30 years of experience in audit, financial and strategic planning, operational excellence, digital transformation, and corporate governance across industries including mining and metals, energy,
technology, and consumer products. Mr.&nbsp;Butler spent 29 years with Ernst&nbsp;&amp; Young LLP (EY) in Arizona, most recently serving as Managing Partner from 2008 until his retirement in 2024. From 2022 to 2024, he also served as EY&#8217;s U.S.
Mining&nbsp;&amp; Metals Leader, where he led national strategy and drove client and business growth, advising major mining companies such as Freeport-McMoRan and Newmont Corporation. As Managing Partner, Mr.&nbsp;Butler led EY Arizona&#8217;s
growth initiatives and strategic ventures, including public-sector programs focused on cost reduction, grants management, real estate optimization, and technology enablement. He also served on the Executive Committee for the City of Phoenix&#8217;s
US$500&nbsp;million General Obligation Bond Program and was a senior member of EY&#8217;s West Region Executive Leadership Team. During his tenure, he oversaw more than 500 professionals and advised a broad range of midsize and multinational public
and private companies. Mr.&nbsp;Butler holds a BSc in Accountancy from the University of Arizona. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Michael Jalonen </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Michael Jalonen is a Chartered Financial Analyst (CFA) with nearly 40 years of mining and capital markets experience, including over 30 years as a highly
respected mining analyst at Bank of America Securities (BofA). He served as Managing Director and North American Senior Precious Metals Research Analyst until his retirement in 2022 and was consistently ranked among the leading mining analysts in
North America. In this role, Mr.&nbsp;Jalonen led coverage and investment recommendations for 30 senior and intermediate precious metals producers, as well as royalty and streaming companies. He developed detailed operating
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 of 3 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
and financial models, performed valuation analyses, and authored numerous thematic industry reports. Prior to that, Mr.&nbsp;Jalonen served as Global Coordinator for BofA&#8217;s Metals,
Mining&nbsp;&amp; Steel Research Team, overseeing a global group of analysts, publishing thematic research on precious and base metals, and organizing the firm&#8217;s flagship global mining conference. He began his career as a geologist.
Mr.&nbsp;Jalonen holds an MBA in Finance from the DeGroote School of Business and a BSc (Hons) in Geology from the University of Windsor. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Steven
Yopps </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Steven Yopps is a metallurgical engineer and accomplished mining executive with more than 35 years of operational, technical, project
development, and regulatory experience across Nevada&#8217;s premier gold districts. His career spans senior roles at AngloGold Ashanti, Nevada Gold Mines, and Barrick Mining, where he led large-scale autoclave, roaster, and refractory processing
operations, advanced complex feasibility studies, and executed district-level growth strategies that transformed regional mining portfolios. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Most
recently, Mr.&nbsp;Yopps served as Vice President of Nevada Projects for AngloGold Ashanti through to his retirement in 2025. In this role, he led technical and exploration teams who were responsible for growing the Nevada resource base, advancing
the feasibility study and NEPA permitting for the North Bullfrog project, and supporting the integration of acquisitions within the Beatty district to establish a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> mining district in southern Nevada.
Previously, Mr.&nbsp;Yopps was Manager of Growth Projects for Nevada Gold Mines (&#8220;NGM&#8221;), where he led the long-term processing and refractory ore transportation strategy following the Newmont&#8211;Barrick joint venture, multiple <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-feasibility</FONT> studies at Cortez, and refractory ore research and development programs. He has authored peer-reviewed research on Carlin-type refractory gold processing and pressure oxidation technologies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prior to his role at NGM, he spent more than 25 years in senior technical and operational roles, including serving as General Manager of the Ruby Hill Mine
(currently <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT> Gold&#8217;s wholly owned Ruby Hill property) and managing Goldstrike&#8217;s autoclave, roaster, and mill facilities for more than a decade, delivering <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> safety and operational performance. Mr.&nbsp;Yopps holds a BSc and MSc in Metallurgical Engineering from the Colorado School of Mines and is a Qualified Person recognized by the
Mining&nbsp;&amp; Metallurgical Society of America. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT> Gold Corp. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT> Gold Corp. is a Nevada-focused mining company committed to building a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-tier</FONT> gold producer through a new development plan to advance its high-quality asset portfolio. The Company is the fourth largest gold mineral resource holder in the state with a pipeline of high-grade
development and production-stage projects strategically located in Nevada&#8217;s most prolific gold-producing trends. Leveraging its central processing facility following an anticipated refurbishment, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT>
Gold is executing a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">hub-and-spoke</FONT></FONT> regional mining and processing strategy to maximize efficiency and growth. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">i-80</FONT> Gold&#8217;s
shares are listed on the Toronto Stock Exchange (TSX:IAU) and the NYSE American (NYSE:IAUX). For more information, visit <U>www.i80gold.com</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 of 3 </P>
